I usually dont base my doctor choice on ratings but I couldn't stop myself from reading all the amazing reviews on Dr. Faraz. I work in a medical clinic myself and the only time I can get to appointments is during lunch before work or after (which most offices dont offer these appointment times). I was very surprised to learn that Dr. Faraz offered appointment time during your normal "lunch hours". I booked my appointment online at 12pm noon and was contacted immediately by email. The first date I requested wasnt available but I was very pleased at the immediate response in the office in letting me know this and offering me another convenient appointment day and time (1 week Later). I filled out my ppwk beforehand because their new patient ppwk is all online. I loved the constant reminders of my appointment (text, email, and phone call). I was even offered to fill out forms of my history online. As soon as I got to the office, the receptionist greeted me very nicely and I felt at ease instantly. The medical Assistant (I'm horrible with names but I think it was debbie) was very courteous and respectful in bringing me back. She acknowledged that I was on my lunch break and would inform the doctor as well. I didnt wait long until Dr Faraz came in, perhaps 10 min IF that.
